href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg" class="image"><img alt="Flag of the United Kingdom.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/32px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="32" height="16" class="noviewer" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/64px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a> <a href="/wiki/Portal:United_Kingdom" title="Portal:United Kingdom">United Kingdom&#32;portal</a>  <div class="hlist" style="text-align:center;font-weight:normal;">\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Outline_of_political_science#Politics_by_region" title="Outline of political science">Other countries</a></li>\n<li><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Atlas_of_the_United_Kingdom" class="extiw" title="commons:Atlas of the United Kingdom">Atlas</a></li></ul>\n</div></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Template:Politics of the United Kingdom"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Template talk:Politics of the United Kingdom"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Her Majesty\'s Most Honourable Privy Council</b>, usually known simply as the <b>Privy Council of the United Kingdom</b> or just the <b>Privy Council</b>, is a <a href="/wiki/Privy_council" title="Privy council">formal body of advisers</a> to the <a href="/wiki/British_monarchy" class="mw-redirect" title="British monarchy">Sovereign</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>. Its membership mainly comprises <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Politics of the United Kingdom">senior politicians</a>, who are current or former members of either the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">House of Commons</a> or the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Lords" title="House of Lords">House of Lords</a>.\n</p><p>The Privy Council formally advises the sovereign on the exercise of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_prerogative_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Royal prerogative in the United Kingdom">Royal Prerogative</a>, and corporately (as <a href="/wiki/Queen-in-Council" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen-in-Council">Queen-in-Council</a>) it issues <a href="/wiki/Executive_(government)" title="Executive (government)">executive instruments</a> known as <a href="/wiki/Order_in_Council" title="Order in Council">Orders in Council</a>, which among other powers enact <a href="/wiki/Act_of_Parliament" title="Act of Parliament">Acts of Parliament</a>. The Council also holds the delegated authority to issue <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Council" title="Order of Council">Orders of Council</a>, mostly used to regulate certain public institutions. The Council advises the sovereign on the issuing of <a href="/wiki/Royal_Charter" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Charter">Royal Charters</a>, which are used to grant special status to incorporated bodies, and <a href="/wiki/City_status_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="City status in the United Kingdom">city</a> or <a href="/wiki/Borough" title="Borough">borough</a> status to local authorities. Otherwise, the Privy Council\'s powers have now been largely replaced by its executive committee, the <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Cabinet of the United Kingdom">Cabinet of the United Kingdom</a>.\n</p><p>Certain judicial functions are also performed by the Queen-in-Council, although in practice its actual work of hearing and deciding upon cases is carried out day-to-day by the <a href="/wiki/Judicial_Committee_of_the_Privy_Council" title="Judicial Committee of the Privy Council">Judicial Committee of the Privy Council</a>. The Judicial Committee consists of <a href="/wiki/List_of_Lords_Justices_of_Appeal" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Lords Justices of Appeal">senior judges</a> appointed as Privy Counsellors: predominantly <a href="/wiki/Justice_of_the_Supreme_Court_of_the_United_Kingdom" class="mw-redirect" title="Justice of the Supreme Court of the United Kingdom">Justices</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Supreme Court of the United Kingdom">Supreme Court of the United Kingdom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Senior_judge" class="mw-redirect" title="Senior judge">senior judges</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a>. The Privy Council formerly acted as the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_court" title="Supreme court">High Court of Appeal</a> for the entire <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> (other than for the United Kingdom itself), and continues to hear <a href="/wiki/Appeal" title="Appeal">appeals</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Crown_Dependencies" class="mw-redirect" title="Crown Dependencies">Crown Dependencies</a>, the <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">British Overseas Territories</a>, and some independent Commonwealth <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Member states of the Commonwealth of Nations">states</a>.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#History"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span term</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#Composition"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Composition</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-4"><a href="#Privy_Council_oath_and_initiation_rite"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Privy Council oath and initiation rite</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-5"><a href="#Term_of_office"><span class="tocnumber">5</span> <span class="toctext">Term of office</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-6"><a href="#Meetings"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Meetings</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-7"><a href="#Functions"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">Functions</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-8"><a href="#Committees"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">Committees</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-9"><a href="#Notable_orders"><span class="tocnumber">9</span> <span class="toctext">Notable orders</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10"><a
